<script id="deposit-launch" type="text/javascript">
        

    $(document).ready(function() {
   
        //find the container
        var _container = $('.deposit-container');
        if( _container.size() == 0 )
        {
            $('<div class="deposit-container"></div>').appendTo($('body'));
            _container = $('.deposit-container');
        }
            
        var inline = _container.hasClass('deposit-inline');
             
        $('.deposit-launch').each( function(){
            	 
            $(this).bind('click', function(event){
                var config = {
                       url: "/eco/teller/deposit.ajax",
                       mode: inline ? '' : 'modal'
                };
                var deposit = new Deposit(_container[0], config);
                deposit.init();
            });	 
        });    
   });

function doLaunchDeposit( )
  {
      var  container = $('.deposit-container');
      if (container.size() == 0) {
             $('<div class="deposit-container"></div>').appendTo($('body'));
             container = $('.deposit-container');
     }
      var config = {
             url: "/eco/teller/deposit.ajax",
             mode: 'modal'
      };
      var deposit = new Deposit(container, config);
      deposit.init();
  }

   </script>

	function iOSversion() {
		if (/iP(hone|od|ad)/.test(navigator.platform)) {
			var v = (navigator.appVersion).match(/OS (\d+)_(\d+)_?(\d+)?/);
			return [parseInt(v[1], 10), parseInt(v[2], 10), parseInt(v[3] || 0, 10)];
		}
	}
	var iOSversion = iOSversion();
	if (iOSversion && iOSversion[0] < 8) {

<script type="text/javascript">
var getUrl = function() {
    return decodeURIComponent(window.location.pathname);
};

var getRefer = function() {
    return document.referrer;
};

var referRegExBM = new RegExp( "(belmont\.ag)" );
var referRegExAH = new RegExp( "(allhorseracing\.ag)" );
var referRegExGH = new RegExp( "(gohorsebetting\.ag)" );

if( getUrl() == "/sbk/sportsbook4/home.sbk" ) {
    if ( referRegExBM.test( getRefer() ) ){
        $("#bm-header").show();
        $("body").css("padding-top", "170px");
    } 
	else if ( referRegExAH.test( getRefer() ) ){
        $("#ahr-header").show();
        $("body").css("padding-top", "170px");
    }
	else if ( referRegExGH.test( getRefer() ) ){
        $("#ghb-header").show();
        $("body").css("padding-top", "170px");
    }
}
$("#bm-close").click( function(){
    $("body").removeAttr("style");
});
$("#ahr-close").click( function(){
    $("body").removeAttr("style");
});
$("#ghb-close").click( function(){
    $("body").removeAttr("style");
});
</script>

 	function loadMBJ() {
 
 	 var sportType = $.cookie("ruibj");
 	 var mbjGameUrl = getMiniBJURLBySport(sportType )['miniBJUrl'];
 	 $("#bj-url").html('<iframe src="' + mbjGameUrl + '" allowtransparency="true" name="miniframe" id="miniframe" width="100%" height="200" frameborder="0" scrolling="no"  marginheight="0" marginwidth="0"></iframe>');
 
 	}
 
 	function getMiniBJURLBySport() {
 	   var sportType = $.cookie("ruibj");
 		var gameUrl = jsonMiniBJURLMap[sportType];
 		var imageUrl = jsonMiniBJImageMap[sportType];
 		
 		
 		if(typeof gameUrl == 'undefined'){
 			gameUrl = jsonMiniBJURLMap['default'];
 		}
 		
 		if(typeof imageUrl == 'undefined'){
 			imageUrl = jsonMiniBJImageMap['default'];
 		}
 		
 		var urlArray = new Array();
 		urlArray['miniBJUrl'] = gameUrl;
 		urlArray['miniBJImageUrl'] = imageUrl;
 		
 		return urlArray;
 	}	
 		
 
 	$('#bj-img').attr('src', getMiniBJURLBySport()['miniBJImageUrl']);

var imgArr = new Array("http://www.sportsbook.ag/static/SBK/www.sportsbook.ag/SB_Footer_Casino_Mobile_v1.jpg","https://www.sportsbook.ag/static/SBK/www.sportsbook.ag/SB_Footer_Jackpot_Mobile_v1.jpg"); //sets array of images

var urlArrMob = new Array("https://www.sportsbook.ag/promos/casino#100CasinoMatchBet","https://www.sportsbook.ag/casino/mobile-slots"); //sets array of mobile URL's

function choosePic() {
	randomNum = Math.floor((Math.random() * urlArr.length));
	document.getElementById("rotateImg").src = imgArr[randomNum];
	
	document.getElementById("rotateUrl").href = urlArr[randomNum];
	
}

choosePic();

</script>

<script>
(function(){
	// Only run the scroll function on pages other than SBK to avoid conflicts with existing scroll up functions on "Betting Engine" page.
	pathnameNonSplitted = window.location.pathname;
	pathname = pathnameNonSplitted.split( '/' );
	var secondLevelLocation = pathname[1]; // SBK

    // SCROLL UP FUNCTION TO SHOW/HIDE ELEMENT FOR PAGES EXCEPT BETTING ENGINE
	if(secondLevelLocation != 'sbk') 
    {    
        $(document).scroll(function() 
        {
            var y = $(this).scrollTop();
            if (y > 600) {
                $('.top-all').fadeIn();
            } else {
                $('.top-all').fadeOut();
            }
        });

		$("footer").on("click", ".top-all", function(event) 
		{
		    event.preventDefault();  
		    $("html, body").animate({scrollTop: 0}, "slow");
		    return false;
		});    
    } 
})();
</script>
